< text>
Our family has lived in Irvine for over 10 years, and this is by far our favorite park for our littles.  My children are 8 years old and 4 years old.  A girl and a boy.  When we make it a park day, these 2 tend to spread out and gravitate to different activities.  What I love about Parasol Park is the size of the vicinity, the fact that it's fairly flat - so there's not many innies & outies and you can easily keep track of your children, and lastly the awesome zip line!
The zip line is really a highlight.  Kids young and older, and even adults, get a kick out of riding the zip line!  I have to admit, it's super fun!
Also, the picnic and eating areas are so charming and always very clean.
Bathrooms are also very well kept and clean.
I also adore the sweet garden area!
Best. Park. Ever!!!< /text>

< review>
Went here as a result of online reviews for a business dinner. Great experience. The restaurant is located in a quiet 'old downtown' area with easy parking and many cute shops. Good craft beer selections and nice wine offerings. They have a fixed price menu and standard menu choices.  Both were excellent.  The steak was perfectly seasoned and perfectly cooked. The chef came out during the meal to check on satisfaction.  The wait staff was extremely attentive without interrupting. We left extremely satisfied. It is not a budget restaurant, but when you want a nice meal, in a nice setting, with good service and good food, this is definitely a place to put near the top of your list.< /review>

<rate>5<//rate><Text>This place is a hidden gem. More people should frequent this restaurant because they do a very nice job and at very affordable prices.

They have items that are are low cost up to high end prime steaks. Their wine list has a nice selection and you can find something at a reasonable price.

Fried Green Bean appetizer was my favorite. not sure how they got that special breading to stay on so well. Served with a sweet tasting aoili which complimented the green beans perfectly.

I had a Prime NY steak and it really was as good as much more expensive steakhouses. Perfectly cooked with the right amount of char. French fries were good, salads were good, soup was a corn choder with crab and it was served piping hot.

Service was outstanding.

I am not sure if Tustin appreciates how well this restaurant executes and how good it is.

These people are trying to hard. It was a bit dead on  a Friday night. Please try this place and I am sure you wll not be disappointed.<//Text><pictures>None<//pictures>< response>
